S=input()

    countI[i]=countI[i+1]+(1 if S[i-1]=='I' else 0)

        mid=1 if c=='J' else (2 if c=='O' else 3)

                            tmp+=1

                        if S[k]=='I':
                            tmp+=1
        if c=='J':

        elif c=='O':

            for i1 in range(pos):
                if S[i1]=='J':
                    tmp += countI[pos+1]
        else:
            tmp= countJ[pos]*countI[pos+1]
        if c=='J':
            tmp=countJ[pos]*countI[pos+1]
        elif c=='O':
            tmp=0
            cntJ=0
            for i1 in range(pos):
                if S[i1]=='J':
                    cntJ+=1
            cntI=0
            for i2 in range(pos,N):
                if S[i2]=='I':
                    cntI+=1
            tmp=cntJ*cntI

            tmp=countJ[pos]*countI[pos+1]
        res=max(res,tmp)
